## Q1 — How many occurrences are on GBIF?

After filtering to kingdom **Plantae**, Christopher Davidson’s GBIF
download contains **26562 occurrences**.

Each occurrence is directly accessible at
`https://www.gbif.org/occurrence/<gbifID>`.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

> The vast majority of occurrences come from **TROPICOS** and **RSA -
> California Botanic Garden Herbarium** (21060 combined). TROPICOS also
> acts as a data aggregator: 9436 occurrences are listed there but not
> physically deposited at MO.

## Q4 — Are digital images available online?

Of 26562 GBIF plant occurrences, **15236 (57.4%) have digital images**
linked on GBIF.

## Q5 — How many unique collections are represented?

| Metric                            | Value |
|-----------------------------------|-------|
| Unique collections                | 15774 |
| Occurrences missing record number | 508   |

> Multiple GBIF occurrences per collection indicate **duplicate
> specimens** distributed across herbaria.

## Q8 — Linking FotW images with SRP specimens

SRP specimen images are not on GBIF but are accessible via the
[Consortium of Pacific Northwest
Herbaria](https://www.pnwherbaria.org/). The local file
`Consortium_PacificNorthWest_herbaria/CPNWH_20250520-112502.csv` lists
all Davidson SRP collections with their accession numbers and an
`Imaged?` flag.

Image URL pattern (accession must be zero-padded to 6 digits):

    https://www.pnwherbaria.org/images/jpeg.php?Image=SRP<ACCESSION>.jpg
    # Example: https://www.pnwherbaria.org/images/jpeg.php?Image=SRP034726.jpg

------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Q9 — Overlap between FotW and GBIF

Records are matched on a composite key: **numeric record number +
collection date** (e.g., `12687_2014-10-04`).

**874 GBIF occurrences** correspond to **468 unique FotW records**.

| Institution    | N_occurrences |
